It can be seen here that the period from December 7 to December 27 last year was a period of sharp decline in silver prices. In the two months from December 27 to the most recent, silver prices have gradually stabilized. In the last month (February), New York's silver price has stabilized at 44.79, and the fluctuations in silver prices in London and Mumbai are also very small. In the past few days, the London silver market has been buying a lot by Indian merchants, and there is no sign of further decline in the market price.

Silver Price Prospects and Chinese Currency

The current silver price has temporarily stabilized, but how long can this be maintained? This is a difficult question to answer. According to an analysis by US financial groups, as a kind of understanding measurement, the silver market experts abroad judge that silver prices will not fall excessively in the future, and that the decline below 20 pence will be very slow, because the period of struggle for silver as a political tool has passed, and it will reappear as a commodity. As a commodity, it must maintain a price ratio with other related commodities. From historical statistical research, the silver price should be maintained at around 20 pence. This statement has been insightful in the London silver market situation for the past two months. Although the amount of silver purchased by the United States in London has gradually decreased, the silver price has remained between 21.75 and 19 pence from December 20 to the most recent, which shows that the commodity nature of silver has been established and the world silver market has become quite clear. However, two conditions must be paid attention to. First, if the US silver policy suddenly changes and a huge amount of silver is released, then this statement will not hold. Second, the stability of silver's commodity nature is not permanent. In terms of commodity nature, silver is not as good as nickel. Silver used as decoration will undergo chemical reactions, and silver production is not like other minerals, which can stop mining when supply exceeds demand. Silver is a byproduct and cannot be restricted. Therefore, the final price of silver cannot be measured by historical price ratios.

However, according to the current situation, the judgment that silver prices will no longer fall excessively is credible. Then, what impact will this have on China's currency? On the surface, the stability of silver prices will make overseas silver prices still more than 10% higher than domestic silver prices, then the problem of China's silver outflow will not be completely eliminated in the future. The government's control policies will hardly collect all the silver in the country, nor will it be able to cope with the erosion of certain foreign forces. Will the stability of silver prices harm China's monetary system? This is not the case. We should recognize that the current key to China's monetary problem is not the silver problem, but the foreign exchange problem and the management problem. Smuggling is no longer enough to destroy the new monetary system, and the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank's insistence on buying and selling foreign exchange without restriction is the key. Therefore, the Chinese people can observe the government's recent silver sales with a calm eye. The stability of silver prices is giving China's currency a chance to gradually consolidate.

Review of Last Year's Silver Price Fluctuations 168

— Xie Juzeng

Last year's (1935) silver market fluctuations were the most significant since the ninth year of the Republic (1920). The highest peak reached 36 and a quarter pence, owing to the elimination of the world's silver standard and the disorganization of the silver market.

As for the monthly silver market fluctuations throughout last year, they can be seen in the table below.

At the beginning of the year, the spot price of silver in London was 24.625, and the forward price was 24.75. During January, the market price fluctuated slightly. At that time, the United States had just satisfied its absorption of any surplus silver and did not exert pressure. While Indian speculators were buying, China was selling. Although the economic difficulties of a major property company threatened currencies in the late month, it had little impact on silver prices. In addition, the American Supreme Court's judgment on gold bar transactions had not yet been determined, so the market was very quiet during the first two weeks of January. However, starting from the 14th, due to a sudden need from speculators, the market price gradually rose from the previous day's 24.4375 to 25.6875 on the 28th. During this period, China's equalization fund had made large purchases; the Indian government also announced at the end of the month that the silver import tax was reduced from five annas to two annas. Market price changes in March were more complex, partly due to the movement of the pound-dollar exchange rate. The main changes occurred between the 22nd and 26th. Because speculators heard that the US Senate had passed Thomas's amendment to the work relief bill, believing that the government would greatly expand the silver purchasing program, they scrambled to buy, so the market price rose by 1.6875. The case was immediately overturned by the House of Representatives, and as a result, the silver price fell by 0.4335. At that time, the US government was buying, China was selling, and speculators in India and London were varying in their buying and selling, so the market situation did not change. In the first week of April, the news of US silver purchases was quiet, and the market price remained below 28.5. On the 9th, the US government resumed purchases, which triggered new buying in China and India. As a result, the market price rose to 28.9375 on the 10th. On the same day, the US government also increased the domestic silver price from US$0.645 to US$0.7111, so the market price rose by 2.379 from the 10th to the 12th to 31.3125. Below this level, many appeared to be profiting, and the sellers of various Chinese banks were quite substantial, so the market price returned to 30.75. After Easter, various parties were confused by the various declarations of the silver group, and those engaged in this business in the East bought unlimitedly at a high price, so the market price rose from 30.9375 on the 18th to 36.25 on the 26th, which was the highest record of the year. On the 24th, the US government increased the domestic silver price from US$0.7111 to zero, US$0.7757, which was equal to 35 pence in London, while the official market price in the British capital was 32.8125. Moreover, there were rumors in the United States that the domestic silver price would gradually increase to US$1.29, and the difference between the world silver price and it would not be very far at that time. This stimulated buying, and buyers were even willing to offer up to 37 pence on the afternoon of April 26.

At that time, Mexico was very worried about this situation and urgently appealed to Washington, believing that if all the currency of the country was absorbed out of the country, the harm would be immeasurable; because the United States continued to implement the policy of raising silver prices, it would drive all the silver in the countries still using the silver standard out of the country, as the US silver purchasing program would be completed one day, leading to this. Subsequently, the United States announced a ban on the import of silver coins, and added an interpretation the next day, the market price fell by .75 to 32.9375. It was then learned that the silver purchasing bill was not related to this, and the market price returned to 33.5625 at the end of the month. At this time, the US government was not very active in the silver market, so transactions were limited to speculation. On June 4, it fell by one pence, and the US Treasury Department began to join the buyers. On the 19th, it fell by another half a pence, and India sold a lot, and transactions were very active. This sale of Indian silver, as well as the supply from Chinese and London speculators, continued until the end of the month. However, the purchasing power of the United States was not strong, so the market price gradually fell to 30 pence.

Earlier, when the market price fluctuated between 36.25 and 32.375 at the turn of April and May, the long positions that were operating were all due in late June and early July. Investors were unwilling to settle the swap for two months. Therefore, on the morning of July 5 (Saturday), India sold a lot and scrambled to settle, and the market price was almost out of control. The broker's market price only fell slightly by 0.3125 to 30.6875, and the US government purchased 10 million ounces at this price. In the following days, it once returned to outside, until August 10, there was no change. The transactions were quiet, and there were occasional speculators engaged in settlement, and the only buyer was the US government.

On August 12, the market situation changed again, and by the 15th it had fallen from 30.1875 to 29 pence. At that time, the US Treasury Department lowered the price by 0.0625, probably because of the soft entanglement of the US rest exchange rate. This caused a huge amount of selling in China and India, and the volume of transactions exceeded the previous records of the year. According to Washington, the US government purchased 25.5 million ounces of silver in London on the 14th alone. The spot market price on the 15th added .0625, which was the first time since August 10, 1934. Since then, until December 7, the US government has not changed the US dollar purchase price. The fluctuations in the London market price were only limited to the rise and fall of the erratic exchange rate. At that time, the US government continued to absorb spot silver supplied from various places, and Hong Kong was the main seller. On August 23, the spot market price suddenly rose to 29.14375, and the futures price was 29.375, but this was only because of the temporary need for forward placements in China and India, and the spot market price was only slightly affected. When the need disappeared, the selling trend returned. In early October, with the outbreak of the Italo-Ethiopian War, the British exchange rate weakened, and speculators once needed it. The spot market price rose to 29.625 on the 5th, and the futures price was 29.75, but it changed to 29.3115 on the 17th. Until November 22, the US purchase price remained unchanged. Then, as the US demand gradually decreased, and Hong Kong and other places continued to abandon, this price was reduced by 0.4375 on November 2.

At the same time, China's financial finance was increasingly disturbed by the impact of the US silver purchasing program. The Shanghai exchange rate was one shilling, six and sixty-eighths pence on October 1, and fell to one shilling, two and seven-eighths pence on November 2. The Hong Kong exchange rate also showed the same change. On November 4, the central government announced the abandonment of the silver standard, the adoption of currency management, the nationalization of silver, and the fixing of the currency value at one shilling, two and a half pence. The banknotes of the Bank of China, Bank of Communications, and Central Bank were used as legal tender to replace silver dollars. The Hong Kong government also followed suit by banning silver exports, but this move had little impact on the entire silver market except for curbing Chinese silver sales. On December 5, the Hong Kong government abandoned the silver standard, and all measures were the same as those implemented by China in mid-November. For the next two days, the silver market seemed indifferent to it. But on the 9th, due to the sudden change of hands in the United States, London brokers did not reach an agreement with the US authorities until the afternoon to suppress the market price by 0.4375. The next day, a huge amount of silver was sold, but the buyers were silent, and the market price could not be determined. This situation was something that had not been seen since the outbreak of the European War in July of the 3rd year of the Republic (1914). Since then, the silver market has not had any overdue transactions. As for the market price, it fell from 29.1875 on the 7th to 20.875 on the 24th. Fortunately, the December transactions were still able to be settled safely, which was still satisfactory.

It is also necessary to describe the situation of US silver purchases in London. From mid-August to the beginning of December, the US authorities sent daily silver purchase entrustment forms to the British capital, with a clear understanding that the London market price must not be stipulated below the US silver price. At that time, the British side firmly adhered to this. Until the first week of December, the United States changed to buying silver elsewhere, and the quantity purchased from London was less than that purchased elsewhere. This sudden change of policy plunged the silver market into chaos for a while. When US Treasury Secretary Morgenthau issued a statement, explaining the reason why the United States changed its policy, the situation became a little clearer. The first thing was to reject the general speculators, because these people used the purchases of the United States as the basis for transactions. But the most important thing that prompted the United States to change its policy was that China abandoned the silver standard.

According to statistics, the United States purchased nearly 390 trillion ounces of silver in the British capital last year, an increase that cannot be underestimated compared with the 86 trillion in 1934. At the end of 1934, the United States had gold reserves of approximately 8,238,000,000 yuan. Silver was calculated at 1.29 yuan per ounce. According to estimates, the United States should purchase at least 1,596 trillion ounces of silver in order to obtain 25% of the silver reserves to stand against 75% of the gold reserves. However, in 1935, the United States still absorbed a lot of gold, so the ratio naturally increased accordingly. The numbers of gold and silver reserves in the United States last year are as follows (unit: million):

From this, it can be seen that although the United States purchased a huge amount of 470 trillion ounces of silver last year, the amount it used to offset the difference was only 180 trillion ounces, and it happened to be in a year when many selling households were tied up, and it was still unable to satisfy its desires; however, recently (February 22, 1936) Washington telegrams stated that the leader of the silver faction has given up any hope of further raising the status of silver in this session of Congress; because on the one hand, the inflation faction is eager to inflate the currency, on the other hand, the US Treasury Department lacks interest in raising silver prices, and on the third hand, the prices of metals such as copper, aluminum, and zinc cannot be raised for one day, then the mining of US silver mines is naturally difficult to be profitable, and even if there is any bill, it will be in vain, so general observations also believe that silver is no longer an important issue.

As for last year, the Indian government sold 20 trillion ounces of silver; Russia sold 16 trillion ounces; Portugal seems to have stopped buying silver, and there was not much buying and selling in other countries in mainland China, but the silver exported by Japan accounted for as much as 85.5 trillion ounces. Seven ounces of this were produced from Japanese silver mines, and most of the rest was smuggled from China.

Chunqiu (Spring and Autumn)

Snippets 174

— (Rong Yu)

One should strive to be a good person; everyone should strive to do good deeds. But if one only wishes to be the sole good person, and only wishes to be the sole doer of good deeds, then that person is the worst in the world.

A man visiting prostitutes and a woman committing adultery are essentially the same. Society harshly condemns women for adultery, but views men visiting prostitutes as commonplace. This is also a distorted view.

The only thing that makes a person willing to be brave and sacrificial is the pursuit of love. If that spirit were applied to other endeavors, nothing would be impossible.

People can cooperate in a leaky boat to reach the shore. But our national character is such that upon seeing the boat leaking and waves coming, everyone blames the captain, while folding their arms and waiting to be buried in the belly of the fish.

Those who can talk but cannot do are the most useless people in the world. Those who can talk and can do are useful. Those who do not talk but bury themselves in hard work are remarkable figures in the world.

Someone Told Me 175

— Zhu Ying

Someone told me, "The taste of a cigarette is best when it's just lit, and when it's about to burn your lips. When it's just lit, the smoke is mellow, and there seems to be a bit of sweetness on the tongue. When it's about to burn your lips, you feel like there's still some taste left over. The most boring part is the middle section, tasteless to eat, a pity to discard."

Someone told me that to write a great article, the beginning must have a few earth-shattering sentences to grab the reader's attention. So, if the beginning of a writing does not have an astonishing opening, it should be discarded and rewritten. At the end of the full text, one also needs to concentrate on using an odd pen to complete it in one breath, so that the reader pats the table and calls it excellent. The middle section is always sloppy, so reading the article the most tasteless part is the middle section.

Someone told me, "In a 10,000-meter race, the first few hundred meters are extremely important, because being at the front at the beginning has the momentum of gaining the upper hand. After 9,000 meters, the trophy is already in sight, and at this time, everyone knows in their feet that they cannot relax. In the middle, although it may not be tense, it is still a bit different. Therefore, to watch a 10,000-meter race, it is enough to watch only the beginning and the end."

Someone told me, "The most inspiring thing about separation is the beginning and the end. At the station, there are always some reluctant farewells, especially the separation of young men and women, with some even weeping. But when the separation ends and they reunite, the tension of their emotions is naturally difficult to describe. In between these two distances, there will inevitably be the pain of being in two places, but in retrospect, all the sweet, sour, bitter, and spicy flavors seem to be only in the two periods of separation and reunion." Someone told me, "The taste of being newly married is really good." Someone also told me, "The taste of growing old together is really good." But among middle-aged couples, at least six or seven out of ten are at odds with each other, arguing every three days and making a scene every four days.

Cultivation Method of Potted Plum Blossoms (Part 2) 176

— Hu Chuyu

Eradicating Pests

Plum blossoms have many pests. For example, scale insects easily breed on tender leaves. Leaves infested by scale insects will curl up. When you see them, you can pour insecticide on them. But the most frightening thing for potted plum blossoms is the larvae of plum moths. These insects specialize in eating plum buds. After the plum buds sprout in the spring, they are almost completely eaten. The insect's body is four to five fen long. Its back is dark brown, its abdomen is red, and it is similar in color to the bark of the plum tree. It has short hairs and yellow stripes. It lurks between the branches and trunks of the plum tree, or in the middle of the bark. When the weather warms up in the spring, it becomes very active. It is often harmed by these insects, causing the plum blossom to wither and die. The mature pupae of these insects are from late April to early May. By early June, they turn into moths and fly to the plum leaves to lay eggs. When there are leaves, they eat the leaves. After the leaves fall, they gnaw on the bark. When the buds sprout, they specialize in eating the buds. Therefore, when the plum leaves grow in the autumn, you must carefully check the leaf surface. Once pests are discovered, use insecticide to eliminate them to prevent them from breeding. There is also a kind of core insect. This insect specializes in eating tender buds when the new shoots elongate in early summer. It is extremely small and is a green, slender beetle. There is also a kind of plum lice, which lies on the leaves. It looks like millet. After the plum leaves are infested by this insect, the front of the leaves turns into white light spots. Ordinary insecticides will not kill them. Sulfur mixture must be used to drive them away. These insects specialize in sucking the nutrients in the leaves, which is very harmful. Plum lovers should pay special attention to this.

Plum Sapling Propagation Method

Plum blossoms are propagated in three ways: seedling cultivation, grafting, and cutting. Potted plum blossoms, if seedling cultivated, can live for eighteen to twenty years. Grafting requires specialized skills. Cutting and seedling cultivation takes several years before they can be transplanted into pots for cultivation. The cutting method is best done around the spring equinox, but it varies depending on the region. Generally, cutting when the flowers have fallen and the leaf buds are gradually expanding is easier to survive. The cuttings should be from last year's new shoots, and they should be selected from those that have been fully exposed to sunlight, with branches that are long and curved. Cut them into five or six inches long, and cut the cut with a sharp knife in one stroke, so that the cut is not crushed. If you use scissors to crush it, it will rot and will not germinate. Also, if the plum cutting is too short, it will not easily survive, and the roots that grow will be poor. The seedling bed for cuttings should be made of soil with a lot of red earth, and it should not have water accumulation. The soil should be three or four inches deep. If you make a seedling bed in the corner of the garden, you can first dig the soil one or two feet deep, repeatedly digging it up, so that the soil is soft. Mix red earth and sand on top to make the water easily penetrate and maintain appropriate humidity. After cutting, it will grow one or two feet tall by autumn. By the spring of the second year, you can prune it to your liking and replant it, but you should fertilize it fully this year. Generally, it is expected to bloom after three years. If the cutting method is correct, it is better than grafting, because the grafting interface often expands, which is very unsightly. Cutting is the same as seedling cultivation, which can avoid this shortcoming.

Chapter Twenty-Four: Greed Over Beauty, The Vulgar Man Reluctantly Gives Up; Ambition High, The Strong Man Walks Away

Hai laughed and said, "Mr. Cheng, you may have misunderstood my meaning. If I had the ability, I wouldn't talk about marriage issues. Rambling Talk

Impressions of the Soviet Print Exhibition 178

— Yang Jinhao

The painting of the Soviet Union for the socialist reality is exhibiting new content and new technology.

In the Second Soviet Print Exhibition in China held by the Youth Association, I met Beihong.

"Their performances are indeed real. Of course, we also need imagination, but it must be based on reality..." he said to me like this.

However, their reality shows differences in subject matter and technology because of the difference between social life and capitalist countries.

The people of the Soviet Union, because of their fighting power, have gradually turned from hearing to nature, because artists who have become a special class have been transformed into common life-longers of the people, because individuals have broken away from all traditional viewpoints. With the restraint, the skills are freely developed. Therefore, they are separated from the current art world of various countries, and the wonderful flowers that are different from the crowd grow.

The reason why woodcuts have achieved results in the Soviet Union is because in that society full of vitality, there is a need for such simple and powerful works to satirize, inspire, and stimulate the general public. Like "Essays" with a sense of battle, they are advanced artistic sketches.

Here, in addition to woodcuts, some watercolors, pencils, monotype, and ink colors aroused my greater attention.

Technically, the overall movement of various painting tools has broken through the difficulties of single tools in expression. This technique of abandoning traditional expression methods has obviously achieved a high degree of success. They not only use brushes, but also use pencils, pens, and even engraving knives at the same time. As long as it is convenient to paint, various techniques can be adopted without being restricted by a certain range. This is the true victory of creative needs. Like the wounded bird made by Bato using the monotype painting method, the wings of a bird struggling with misfortune and the feathers of each part, the precise brush strokes cannot be drawn by simple oil painting or watercolor. Furthermore, the mechanization of bridge construction made by Lei Te also uses steel pens and watercolors at the same time. The crane on the shore of the Nepalese River made uses pencil lines in addition to watercolor. This painting method adapts to today's improved printing technology.

In spirit, we cannot see the themes of enjoyment or worry there. What they draw are some lively, heavy, and fighting expressions. For example, the football made by Antonov expresses the lively and healthy life of Soviet teenagers. The Cultural Rest Park made by Kashinga expresses the entertainment of the Soviet people, and at the same time instills healthy cultural knowledge. In particular, many descriptions of mechanical engineering, such as the construction of the Nepalese river water gate and the installation of boilers made by Dolmichetoff, and the preparation for the launch of wooden boats in the shipyard made by Pavloff, etc., show the Soviet Union's socialistic construction movement. The active and diligent, and the general public’s clear understanding of this kind of work and deep interest make the artists who are pioneers integrated into this kind of life, truly sincerely and powerfully write realistically on a wide range, and become encouraging and promoting This kind of painting that grasps great historical traces gives the public the excitement to step up their efforts.

However, this kind of painting cannot and cannot be produced in other countries where the air is full of economic panic, the disease of depression and pain is prevalent, the labor of the labor is ignored, and the artistic writers do not have this kind of real feeling. Only in the Soviet Union, where the Five-Year Plan has been successfully completed and is continuing, and only in the Soviet Union, where class status has been eliminated and all the people have become a whole creative force, does Tao have this victorious condition.

There are also many portraits, landscapes, illustrations, and historical sounds, etc., which are vigorous, magnificent, relaxed, and solemn, but each is full of vitality, and they are all very precious.

Keeping birds in cages is like keeping beauties in golden houses. The size and height of the cage must be configured according to the bird's weaving skills. There are things that cannot be confused. One famous cage maker is Mr. Du of Kunshan, known as Du's cage. Mr. Du was born during the Tongzhi period of the former Qing Dynasty. The cages he made were elegant and not vulgar, which was difficult for writers to achieve. However, after the Red Goat Fire, there are no more left in the market. In the early years of Guangxu, Mei Fenglin's yellow-headed cage in Changshu was also very famous. This cage is suitable for keeping spotted-necked birds, and people scramble to buy it. The Wang cage imitated by Mr. Wang of Fushan only gets its appearance, but it is not as good as it. Zhou Zaichen and his son made twisted silk, ice plum carved flower white-eye cages, which only flaunted their fine carvings and were not worth mentioning. The best of these products should be the Zhifu cage. Zhifu, surnamed Yao, is a native of Wujun. He has a great love for white-eye birds, so he made his own gold wire bamboo cages. The step bow of the cage wire eyes is different in each section, which people cannot imitate. It is a pity that only a few cages were made, and it is difficult to buy them with a lot of money. I heard that Mr. Jiang of Xishan has a Zhifu cage, accompanied by Ling Jushi's hook, ancient kiln jar, and green mother-son pieces. It is ancient and extraordinary. Mr. Jiang regards it as a treasure, and people also see it and sigh with envy. Nowadays, the market is flooded with Jin Sanwei's gold wire cages, which are inferior to the previous ones.

The Duck Knows First When the Spring River Warms 181

— Xie Yun

It was early spring, and the mild sun shone on my body, warming me and making me sleepy. Wearing a cotton robe, I felt a little hot.

The pool of water in front of the building was so lovely with its blue hue. A group of brown ducks floated and sank in the water, swimming back and forth, often submerging their beaks into the water, wagging their tails, and splashing water up and down to wash their bodies. They quacked and chased each other, playing happily. The ripples on the water surface expanded in circles, shaking the reflections of the tree branches in the water, like countless golden snakes wriggling, their shapes extremely happy. The willow branches on the shore were still shaking in the wind, and the shadows of the branches were reflected in the pool, as if they were ashamed and complained about the late arrival of the spring breeze.

Spring has come, and this group of happy ducks was the first to throw themselves into its embrace.

Zhu Chengnian's Thief 184

— Jiawei

According to reports, in a certain lane in Henan Road, Zhabei, there is an empty house that has been sealed by the court. Unexpectedly, one night, a big hole was dug in the wall of the house by a thief, and many things were stolen and moved out. After the North Station Detective Team successively arrested a large number of thieves related to the case, the oldest was only fifteen years old, one person; the remaining three were only thirteen years old, all underage children. One of the receivers of stolen goods was also only eighteen years old. They have now been sent to the General Bureau for disposal.

Illegal incidents involving theft and robbery are, in today's riddled social organization, occurring every day and are on the rise! Isn't it obvious? In the past, there were college students in Shanghai who became thieves and went to jail, and college students in Hangzhou who became robbers and were executed...etc., have become commonplace.

However, among these unscrupulous people who "take without regard for righteousness," I am afraid that most of them are driven by life and oppressed by the economy to take risks, right? Of course, others, like the "idlers who do not engage in proper business" produced in today's social environment, which is a mixture of ancient feudal remnants and corrupt capitalist civilization residue, is also the inevitable next best thing!

However, these are all young and middle-aged people who have reached adulthood. We rarely hear about those thirteen or fourteen-year-old children who plan to commit theft in groups like the ones mentioned above (of course, it is common to see children stealing a pancake or an orange from a vendor's stall; but they will never be as "mature" as these children, right?)

Here, of course, some people will again attribute it to the bankruptcy of today's education. That's right. However, we cannot completely ignore the relationship between education and society, as well as the fundamental reasons for its bankruptcy.

Isn't that right? How long have the cries of "Save the children!" been going on? But what enlightenment has this incident given us?

The "compulsory education" that has been sung for a long time, and even the "compulsory education" that has been implemented for more than half a year, their achievements are probably only these, right?

Sure enough, every week, more cinemas are showing "children's education films," right? However, how many of the films shown have even a little bit of "educational" meaning? Moreover, what is the relationship between these films and street urchins who make a living by stealing?

Well, in short, everything, no matter how great, is ultimately inseparable from this cage of society, right?!

So, if we want to cry "Save the children!", where should we start? Let's all work hard!

Raven Robbery (Continued) 185

— Shen Wu

Dusk. We really are about to leave. Old Man Zhu muttered to himself for a while, saying that chasing crows early in the morning brings bad luck to children; he also trembled about not accumulating good deeds and that one shouldn't harm living creatures casually: killing living beings... This old man, as usual, trembled for a while, then silently packed his belongings, went to burn incense for the Goddess of Mercy, and chanted spells.

This time, the procession was truly impressive. A dozen or so spears, plus Old Yan's and Old Mo's two short guns, marched mightily towards the mountain path. Old Ge rode Hu Datou's jujube horse, straightened his back, and escorted our team, looking even more imposing. The children in the village stared at us with curious eyes until the shadow of the village gradually receded from us.

After passing two steep mountain peaks, bizarre rocks were scattered all over the mountain path, and the weeds grew so tall that they sometimes blocked the way ahead. The mountain path was rugged, making it very difficult to walk. Once we reached the mountain bend, Old Yan's imposing manner had diminished by more than half. He no longer escorted the rear of the team, but gradually squeezed into the middle of the crowd. We were all silent, focusing only on walking along the mountain path.

The sky gradually darkened. The sun sank below the horizon, and the red glow of the sky was reflected in the mountains, creating beautiful mountain scenery. However, this fleeting dusk mountain scenery was quickly swallowed by darkness. Walking in the dark mountains made us feel even more difficulty. Someone turned on a flashlight, and a beam of white light shone brightly, but Old Yan immediately scolded them down. So everyone had to continue groping, stumbling along the rugged mountain path, with boundless darkness ahead.

The mountain path sometimes rose and sometimes fell. Those walking in the vanguard often stumbled several times. This time, after turning a bend in the mountain, the path became low-lying again, the surrounding weeds were very tall, and the rocks were very jagged. The people in the vanguard suddenly fell down, and couldn't get up for a while, as if someone had rolled down. Old Song turned on the flashlight and shone it around, and it seemed that several ropes were stretched across the mountain road. Old Yan was shouting loudly from behind, telling them not to turn on the flashlight. Before the shout stopped, several cold rifle shots rang out. Old Song sensitively turned off the flashlight, Old Yan panicked and didn't know what to do; the horse neighed, and Old Man Zhu also became flustered...

The gunshots became more and more numerous and gradually intensified. Our dozen or so spears finally reached the peak, leaving only a few carrying poles and a horse on the mountain path. However, we couldn't find the enemy's target, so we just fired back a few shots randomly, resisting the enemy's flames.

In the midst of the intense gunfire, someone cried out miserably. The sound was very close to us, and we couldn't help but be startled. Our hearts began to beat strangely. Gradually, in the firelight, we discovered that the enemy had formed an encirclement. Everyone hid between the grass and the rocks, firing back. The gunfire became more and more intense, and the cries of the people became even more tragic. But suddenly we heard the enemy's gunfire gradually fade away, and finally, after coldly answering a few shots, it stopped.

Old Song immediately walked down the mountain path from the shelter of the rocks and shone the flashlight in the direction of the cries. The horse had disappeared. Old Man Zhu lay slowly on the ground, a pool of blood flowing from his thigh. Old Yan was huddled in a ball among the weeds in the mountain bend...

We helped Old Man Zhu up, and someone found some wild yams in the mountains to apply to his wound. He gasped and murmured, "Not accumulating good deeds?... Chasing crows early in the morning!... It's unlucky!... I always said: the children don't listen..."

We didn't say anything, just remained silent. The mountains were still filled with boundless darkness and coldness. The night was still long.

Midnight Street Building 188

— Hua Mu

Occasionally, I stay overnight at a friend's house. The bedroom faces a road. After we're tired of talking and go to sleep, the lights are turned off, and the neon lights on the storefronts on both sides of the road combine to create a colorful light and shadow that flows into the room and is reflected on a painted screen mirror. Seeing this faint and dazzling light and shadow, my heart feels as if it's touched by a slight electric current, and a kind of unspeakable bewilderment floats up; to put it lightly, it's a kind of melancholy feeling, right? I have a habit of disliking beds, so I expected I wouldn't be able to sleep well tonight. However, I don't get annoyed by this. I often feel that insomnia isn't necessarily a painful but delightful thing: half a bed of warm mattress, a long and silent night, allowing people to travel between heaven and earth, east, south, west, and north, creating all kinds of strange and magnificent dreams, or chewing on the traces of joy and sorrow in the process of life. It's much more interesting than falling asleep as soon as one touches the mat. These are all leisure activities that are not easy to enjoy in the midst of the busy daily life.

It's almost midnight. Dazzled by the light and shadow outside the building, although I've taken off my outer clothes, I haven't gone to bed yet. Leaning against a glass window, I crane my neck to look down. On the oily asphalt ground, cars flow past like mercury. The lights shine on the shiny car armor, reflecting a dazzling light. In an instant, it slides past, faintly leaving a shock, with the smell of gasoline floating in the air. This stream flows past, flows back, and weaves into a kind of bustling and noisy sound. It turns out that not far ahead, the tall building that shines in the night sky is a certain dance hall, and this time is when gentlemen and ladies are driving to the banquet. For the past half year, I've mostly lived in the suburbs. I've gradually become unfamiliar with the atmosphere of the city at night. When I lived in the suburbs, I was also in a small building overlooking a village road. Midnight there was only a desolate calmness. Occasionally, a passing pedestrian walks on the fine sand road with a monotonous pace, or there is an unnatural cough, which causes several long dog barks, making people feel that this is completely a remote mountain village, and it never occurs to them that just a few miles away, there is a bustling and luxurious area. In addition, there is the sound of the hawker selling wontons in the wind and rain, slowly and leisurely striking, walking past the door, also with a very strong medieval tone, a kind of peaceful and leisurely fun full of hypnotic qualities, with no trace of erotic stimulation mixed in. I have no love or aversion for such a realm. However, I'm feeling a bit unfamiliar to the erotic bewilderment of the city at night, but after all, I have a sense of intimacy and fusion. Even if I have insomnia, I can only blame it on my habit of disliking beds. This is not a sophism.

Therefore, I feel that the loveliness of Shanghai, which makes people fascinated, is all due to the obvious and strong erotic stimulation woven in the night. If there were no bright and gorgeous lights in the night, adjusting the noisy city sounds and appearances, and the world turned dark and silent at night, even if the daytime was bustling with traffic and noise all day long, it would lose its meaning of prosperity. Living in Shanghai, if you only see the hustle and bustle of the day and do not appreciate the light, color, sound, and interest of the night, then you can only say that you have seen and understood half of Shanghai. Some people often express an exaggerated argument, cursing Shanghai as an uninhabitable demon cave. This is really inevitable, emotional, and overcorrecting. Of course, it is not necessary to say that Shanghai is a paradise on earth, a land of happiness for the rich and poor. It certainly makes people fall, makes people lose their lives, and also provides food for many people's lives: leaving aside good and bad, the merits and demerits are offset. Just take tonight's situation as an example. While I am enjoying the sounds of the cars and the dazzling scenery outside the building in the small building, someone in the neighboring building may be suffering from the noise and lights of this midnight.

Will I really be disturbed by the beauty of this city night and have insomnia? No, that can only be attributed to my habit of disliking beds. If this street building becomes my own, then I can correct it soon. This place can give me a richer and more lively emotion. I envy my friend's happiness, and I also envy the people who have such a street building. I bless Shanghai.

Early Winter in Qingyang Port (6) 189

— Qiu Yuan

At this moment, Qiu Hua appeared before him. This appearance was truly unexpected. It had been a year or two since Zhuo Min first met Qiu Hua. At that time, her uncle accompanied her to the office of a publication that Zhen Min was in charge of. Of course, at that time, he only regarded her as a female student. However, in some conversations, he learned that she was capable of not going with the flow and surpassing her peers; among Chinese painters, she admired Ding Jun alone, and Ding Jun was admired by Zhuo Min. This first impression was enough to be deeply engraved. However, Zhen Min always reminded himself that he was already a married man; although there was a deep first impression, it couldn't withstand the passage of time, and in the end, it faded away.

It was in the summer, a year later in the summer, that he met Qiu Hua again on another occasion. Her conversation was more clever, and her actions were more lively and moving. From her bright eyes, one could also see that there was an unspeakable, but actually not unspeakable, charm hidden inside. However, Zhen Min always felt that he was a married man, and any thoughts had to be quickly dispelled. Moreover, although he was not such an outdated person, feudal morality often lingered in his mind. It was after this occasion that he had to give up everything.

It was in early autumn that her uncle came to Shanghai from X place, and there were several other companions. When they arrived in Shanghai, they had to drink. Among them was a single university professor who was already mature in his mid-thirties, but extremely naive at heart, who was extremely enamored of Qiu Hua. Zhuo Min had known this for a long time, and he hoped that they could soon reach paradise. However, this university professor was too naive after all, he didn't know anything. Because of her, he invited many people to eat together one day. Zhuo Min was there, and Qiu Hua was also there. She was more charming, but in the midst of the laughter of the guests, she was always silent. After the meal, they went to her house, at which time her parents had gone to Qingdao to escape the summer heat, leaving her alone. This group went, and also after drinking, they couldn't help but fool around for a while, some singing songs, some laughing inexplicably, while Zhuo Min sat silently and Qiu Hua also sat listlessly. When the guests were tired and couldn't even open their mouths, Qiu Hua took out her Hawaiian ukulele and played the poignant Hawaiian farewell song, the moving Aabe ol! For Zhuo Min, this farewell song especially made him feel a nameless sadness. This melody suddenly made him think of things that happened eight years ago. The scene of crossing the Pacific to the United States eight years ago, when the ship docked in Honolulu, and what he had experienced in the past eight years, came to mind one by one. Time has passed, and old travels are like dreams. What has he gained in the past eight years? The loneliness of sorrow and the desolation of loneliness have increased year by year with the increase of age. Now, when Qiu Hua plays this moving Hawaiian clear string, how can Zhuo Min not feel sad in secret. So he couldn't help but get up, as if he could use the excuse of being drunk, raise his voice, and sing Western songs one by one...and I Know that someday I'll discover the girl of my vagabond dream. He looked at Qiu Hua, looked at her smile filled with affection, and Zhuo Min realized the meaning of "understanding" for the first time.

Opening "Sister-in-law Teasing"

The girl moves into the boudoir. Bowing deeply to the beauty. Sister-in-law, last night my brother returned home. Did you share the pillow together? What happened last night, so much noise? What were you laughing about? Sister-in-law, as the saying goes, a new marriage is not as good as a long separation. Reunion after a long separation is like honey. Why are you so tired today? Why don't you tell me the details? Girl, stop teasing. Don't make a sound. What was the noise last night? It was a cat catching a mouse, a big fight. I wanted to call you. But your brother begged me not to make a sound. I was angry, annoyed, and amused. So there was a雜亂sound in my room. Sister-in-law, I think when my brother is not home. Why is it so quiet and silent? Can he make the mouse make trouble? Isn't it absurd to say that? Sister listen. Calling girl. This matter is not suitable to say the details. If you want to know the details. Wait for your brother to come back and tell you next door. Don't let your brother know. And don't talk about it behind his back. Sister-in-law, tonight my brother is not home. Come, come, let me represent my brother to成双. Sister-in-law retreated in a hurry. That girl is teasing the beauty in every way. How funny is the young woman in the boudoir. Black-Clothed Heroine, Starring Grande Swarthout 199

Is a Singer with Both Beauty and Talent

There have been several more famous opera singers from the New York Metropolitan Opera who have dedicated themselves to the silver screen. The more famous ones include Grande Moore, Lawrence Tibbett, Mary Alice, and Negomata Tiema. Now there is another popular singer, Grande Swarthout CGMLCYsSwarthout, who plays the lead role in Paramount's new film "Black-Clothed Heroine" Rose of Rancho (the male lead of the film is John Bowers, which will be released soon at the Cathay Cinema), and her beautiful appearance and slender figure have fascinated many young people. Last year, when the United States elected beauty, she was surprisingly selected as the standard beauty of the United States. It is said that Paramount Company spent a lot of effort to invite her to join the film industry this time, which can't but be said to be a feast for the eyes of movie fans.

"National Beauty" to be Released Soon 201

However, the song and dance film "National Beauty" directed by Du Yu has already been completed and will be released soon. The film is divided into ten scenes: Visiting Uncle, Meeting a Woman, Lodging, Selling Candy, Banquet, Emotional Tide, Mistake, Cameo Appearance, Exotic Dance, Resumption of Business. Dan Erchun, who has not appeared on the screen for a long time, plays the role of Fisherman, Bai Hong plays Baozhen, and Bai Yan plays a singer, all of whom are competent. The sets include night markets, lights and shadows, the screen is extremely strange and delightful, and there is also a heavy rain scene, which is extremely grand. The novelty of the filming is unprecedented. Some say that Du Yu is the only smart person in the film industry, and it is expected that there will be a grand scene when it is released.
